# File: region.txt

# This file holds templates for wilderness regions.

# The complete Middle-Earth map is currently 588 miles high by 735 miles wide. 
# y and x coordinates are for the top left of the region as shown in the D:
# lines (so in particular, that does include spaces).
# Each grid represents 1 square mile.
# Each square mile contains 10x10 portions of wilderness of 22x22 game grids,
# called chunks.

# name:region name
# realm:realm it belongs to
# danger:danger level of the region
# height:height of the region map
# width:width of the region map
# y-offset:y offset of the top of the region map
# x-offest:x offset of the left edge of the region map
# D:Map of the region using the following legend:
# * Snow
# + Forest
# , Moor/Waste
# - Lake
# . Plain
# / Desert
# = Town
# X Impassable Mountain
# ^ Mountain
# _ Swamp
# | Dark Forest
# ~ Ocean
